            def pivot(direction='keys',&block)
        
      212. 
      
        
    212. 
          
          
              a=self.class.new
        
      213. 
      
        
    213. 
          
          
              direction=direction.to_s
        
      214. 
      
        
    214. 
          
          
              up=pivot_direction_up?(direction)
        
      215. 
      
        
    215. 
          
          
              each_pair{|k1,v1|
        
      216. 
      
        
    216. 
          
          
                v1.each_pair{|k2,v2|
        
      217. 
      
        
    217. 
          
          
                  k = up ? k1 : k2
        
      218. 
      
        
    218. 
          
          
                  a[k]=[] if (a[k]==nil or a[k]=={})
        
      219. 
      
        
    219. 
          
          
                  a[k]<<(v2)
        
      220. 
      
        
    220. 
          
          
                }
        
      221. 
      
        
    221. 
          
          
              }
        
      222. 
      
        
    222. 
          
          
              if block
        
      223. 
      
        
    223. 
          
          
                a.each_pair{|key,val| a[key]=block.call(val)}
        
      224. 
      
        
    224. 
          
          
              end
        
      225. 
      
        
    225. 
          
          
              a
        
      226. 
      
        
    226. 
          
          
            end
        
      227. 
      
        
    227. 
          
          
          
        
      228.

          1

      229.

          1
          
            def pivot_direction_up?(direction_name)
        
      231. 
      
        
    231. 
          
          
              case direction_name.to_s
        
      232. 
      
        
    232. 
          
          
              when 'key','keys','up','left','out' then return true
        
      233. 
      
        
    233. 
          
          
              when 'val','vals','down','right','in' then return false
        
      234. 
      
        
    234. 
          
          
              else raise ArgumentError.new('Pivot direction must be either: key/keys/up/left/out or val/vals/down/right/in')
        
      235. 
      
        
    235. 
          
          
              end
        
      236. 
      
        
    236. 
          
          
            end

           def self.prev_char(chr) #=> prev_char, changed_flag, carry_flag
        
      128. 
      
        
    128. 
          
          
            case chr
        
      129. 
      
        
    129. 
          
          
            when '1'..'9', 'B'..'Z', 'b'..'z'
        
      130. 
      
        
    130. 
          
          
              pos=(chr.respond_to?(:ord) ? chr.ord : chr[0])
        
      131. 
      
        
    131. 
          
          
              return (pos-1).chr, true, false
        
      132. 
      
        
    132. 
          
          
            when '0'
        
      133. 
      
        
    133. 
          
          
              return '9', true, true
        
      134. 
      
        
    134. 
          
          
            when 'A'
        
      135. 
      
        
    135. 
          
          
              return 'Z', true, true
        
      136. 
      
        
    136. 
          
          
            when 'a'
        
      137. 
      
        
    137. 
          
          
              return 'z', true, true
        
      138. 
      
        
    138. 
          
          
            else
        
      139. 
      
        
    139. 
          
          
              return chr, false, false
        
      140. 
      
        
    140. 
          
          
            end
        
      141. 
      
        
    141. 
          
          
           end
        
      142.

           def prev!
        
      168. 
      
        
    168. 
          
          
            return self if length==0
        
      169. 
      
        
    169. 
          
          
            index=length-1 # rightmost
        
      170. 
      
        
    170. 
          
          
            while true do
        
      171. 
      
        
    171. 
          
          
             chr=self[index].chr
        
      172. 
      
        
    172. 
          
          
             prev_chr,changed_flag,carry_flag=String.prev_char(chr)
        
      173. 
      
        
    173. 
          
          
              return self if !changed_flag
        
      174. 
      
        
    174. 
          
          
             self[index]=prev_chr
        
      175. 
      
        
    175. 
          
          
             return self if !carry_flag
        
      176. 
      
        
    176. 
          
          
             index-=1
        
      177. 
      
        
    177. 
          
          
             return nil if index<0
        
      178. 
      
        
    178. 
          
          
            end
        
      179. 
      
        
    179. 
          
          
            return self
        
      180. 
      
        
    180. 
          
          
           end
